to_check_exarch_accepted_culture = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				OR = {
					to_has_exarch_government_reform = yes
					to_has_independant_exarch_government_reform = yes
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					NOT = { accepted_culture = PREV }
				}
			}
			owner = {
				add_accepted_culture = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_province = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag }
			}
			to_potential_exarch_province = yes
			to_exarch_can_get_province_on_owner_change = yes
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = to_exarch_province_recipient
		}
		to_exarch_effect_from_province = {
			EFFECT = "
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = event_target:to_exarch_province_recipient
					is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
					NOT = { has_country_flag = to_block_exarch_province_transfer }
				}
				save_event_target_as = to_exarch_province_recipient
			}
			"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_saved_event_target = to_exarch_province_recipient
					event_target:to_exarch_province_recipient = {
						is_subject_of = PREV
						is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
						NOT = { has_country_flag = to_block_exarch_province_transfer }
					}	
				}
			}
			to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
				CURRENT_OWNER = owner
				NEW_OWNER = event_target:to_exarch_province_recipient
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_province_colony_finished = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				nhs_check_all_elysian_tags = { CONDITION = tag }
			}
			to_potential_exarch_province = yes
			to_exarch_can_get_province_active = yes
		}
		owner = {
			save_event_target_as = to_exarch_province_recipient
		}
		to_exarch_effect_from_province = {
			EFFECT = "
			if = {
				limit = {
					exists = yes
					is_subject_of = event_target:to_exarch_province_recipient
					is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
					NOT = { has_country_flag = to_block_exarch_province_transfer }
				}
				save_event_target_as = to_exarch_province_recipient
			}
			"
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					has_saved_event_target = to_exarch_province_recipient
					event_target:to_exarch_province_recipient = {
						is_subject_of = PREV
						is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
						NOT = { has_country_flag = to_block_exarch_province_transfer }
					}	
				}
			}
			to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
				CURRENT_OWNER = owner
				NEW_OWNER = event_target:to_exarch_province_recipient
			}
		}
	}
}

to_make_exarch_province_reserved = {
	set_province_flag = to_exarch_province_reserved
	clr_province_flag = nhs_exarch_province_exemption
}

to_remove_exarch_edict_modifiers = {
	remove_country_modifier = to_crack_down_on_heresy
	remove_country_modifier = to_exarch_aid
}

to_check_crack_down_on_heresy_validity = {
	$SCOPE$ = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = to_crack_down_on_heresy
				OR = {
					NOT = { is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject }
					NOT = {
						any_owned_province = {
							NOT = { religion = ROOT }
						}
					}
				}
			}
			remove_country_modifier = to_crack_down_on_heresy
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_aid_cost = {
	$SCOPE$ = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_send_aid_cost
				value = trigger_value:num_of_cities
			}
			[[ADJUST]
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_send_aid_cost
					value = $ADJUST$
				}
			]
			divide_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_send_aid_cost
				value = 5
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_send_aid_cost
				value = 0.001
			}
			round_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_send_aid_cost
				value = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

to_exarch_reform_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = to_reform_effects_for_overlord_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			overlord = {
				mission_completed = to_the_eagle_rises_mission
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_govcap_exarch_reduced_tt
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_forcelimit_exarch_reduced_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_govcap_exarch_tt
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_forcelimit_exarch_tt
	}
	custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_reform_effects_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_automatically_accepts_culture_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_min_autonomy_exarch_modifier_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_province = {
			to_handle_exarch_autonomy_modifier = yes
			if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = {
						NOT = { accepted_culture = PREV }
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					add_accepted_culture = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
	custom_tooltip = to_forced_new_line_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		to_setup_exarch_merchant_counter = yes
		to_imperial_integration_country_check = yes
		to_check_exarch_nationalism = {}
		to_check_exarch_modifier = { MODIFIER_NAME = "coring_cost" MODIFIER = "core_creation" }
		to_check_exarch_modifier = { MODIFIER_NAME = "admin_efficiency" MODIFIER = "administrative_efficiency" }
		to_check_kastrioti_dominion_modifier_all_provinces = yes
	}
}

to_exarch_reform_removed_effect = {
	hidden_effect = {
		to_imperial_integration_country_check = yes
		every_owned_province = {
			remove_province_modifier = to_exarch_autonomy_penalty
		}
		to_remove_exarch_edict_modifiers = yes
		to_remove_exarch_nationalism_modifiers = yes
		to_remove_exarch_coring_cost_modifiers = yes
		to_remove_exarch_admin_efficiency_modifiers = yes
	}
}

to_exarch_reform_independant_effect = {
	custom_tooltip = to_reform_effects_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_automatically_accepts_culture_tt
	hidden_effect = {
		every_owned_province = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = {
						NOT = { accepted_culture = PREV }
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					add_accepted_culture = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_set_initial_exarch_targets = {
	EEH = { save_global_event_target_as = to_EEH_target }
	EEY = { save_global_event_target_as = to_EEY_target }	
}

to_swap_exarch_dynamic_tag = {
	hidden_effect = {
		$NEW_TAG$ = {
			save_global_event_target_as = to_$BASE_TAG$_target
		}
		$BASE_TAG$ = {
			override_country_name = $NEW_NAME$
		}
		$CURRENT_TAG$ = {
			$NEW_TAG$ = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = { has_country_flag = to_block_exarch_second_merchant }
					}
					set_country_flag = to_block_exarch_second_merchant
				}
				else = {
					clr_country_flag = to_block_exarch_second_merchant
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_set_exarch_always_count_for_merchant_province = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			PREV = {
				has_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
			}
		}
		PREV = {
			clr_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
			value = -1
		}
	}
	change_variable = {
		which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
		value = -1
	}
}

to_set_exarch_always_count_for_merchant_2_province = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			PREV = {
				has_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
			}
		}
		PREV = {
			clr_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
			value = -1
		}
	}
	change_variable = {
		which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
		value = -1
	}
}

to_set_exarch_always_count_for_merchant = {
	set_province_flag = to_exarch_always_count_for_merchant
	to_exarch_merchant_effect_from_province = {
		EFFECT = "
		to_set_exarch_always_count_for_merchant_province = yes
		"
	}
	to_exarch_merchant_2_effect_from_province = {
		EFFECT = "
		to_set_exarch_always_count_for_merchant_2_province = yes
		"
	}
}

to_setup_exarch_merchant_counters_province = {
	change_variable = {
		which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
		value = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			PREV = {
				owned_by = PREV
			}
		}
		PREV = {
			set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

to_setup_exarch_merchant_2_counters_province = {
	change_variable = {
		which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
		value = 1
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			PREV = {
				owned_by = PREV
			}
		}
		PREV = {
			set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
		}
		change_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
			value = 1
		}
	}
}

to_setup_exarch_merchant_counters = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = to_setup_exarch_merchant_provinces }
		}
		set_global_flag = to_setup_exarch_merchant_provinces
		to_exarch_effect_including_inactive = {
			EFFECT = "
				set_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
					value = 0
				}
				set_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
					value = 0
				}
				"
		}
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				is_empty = no
				is_colony = no
				OR = {
					continent = europe
					continent = africa
					continent = asia
				}
				NOT = { to_province_always_counts_for_exarch_merchant = yes }
			}
			to_exarch_merchant_effect_from_province = {
				EFFECT = "
				to_setup_exarch_merchant_counters_province = yes
				"
			}
			to_exarch_merchant_2_effect_from_province = {
				EFFECT = "
				to_setup_exarch_merchant_2_counters_province = yes
				"
			}
		}
	}
}

to_fix_exarch_merchant_counters = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			to_has_exarch_government_reform = yes
			OR = {
				is_variable_equal = {
					which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
					value = 0
				}
				AND = {
					to_exarch_has_merchant_land_2 = yes
					is_variable_equal = {
						which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
						value = 0
					}
				}
			}
		}
		to_setup_exarch_merchant_counter = yes
	}
}

to_setup_exarch_merchant_counter = {
	set_variable = {
		which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
		value = 0
	}
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { to_province_always_counts_for_exarch_merchant = yes }
			to_exarch_merchant_land = {
				SCOPE = "PREV"
			}
		}
		PREV = {
			change_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
				value = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					PREV = {
						owned_by = PREV
					}
				}
				PREV = {
					set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			to_exarch_has_merchant_land_2 = yes
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
			value = 0
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
			value = 0
		}
		every_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { to_province_always_counts_for_exarch_merchant = yes }
				to_exarch_merchant_land_2 = {
					SCOPE = "PREV"
				}
			}
			PREV = {
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
					value = 1
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						PREV = {
							owned_by = PREV
						}
					}
					PREV = {
						set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
					}
					change_variable = {
						which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_merchant_counter_all_owned_provinces = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
			value = 0
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { to_province_always_counts_for_exarch_merchant = yes }
				to_exarch_merchant_land = {
					SCOPE = "owner"
				}
			}
			set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
			PREV = {
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				to_exarch_has_two_merchants = yes
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
				value = 0
			}
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { to_province_always_counts_for_exarch_merchant = yes }
					to_exarch_merchant_land_2 = {
						SCOPE = "owner"
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
				PREV = {
					change_variable = {
						which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_merchant_counter = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
			}
			NOT = { has_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { to_province_always_counts_for_exarch_merchant = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					to_exarch_merchant_land = {
						SCOPE = "owner"
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
				owner = {
					change_variable = {
						which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					owner = {
						to_exarch_has_two_merchants = yes
					}
					to_exarch_merchant_land_2 = {
						SCOPE = "owner"
					}
				}
				set_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
				owner = {
					change_variable = {
						which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
			}
			has_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
		}
		clr_province_flag = to_was_counted_for_exarch_merchant
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = { to_exarch_has_two_merchants = yes }
				to_exarch_merchant_land_2 = {
					SCOPE = "FROM"
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant_2
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			FROM = {
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_owned_provinces_for_merchant
					value = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_trigger_exarch_ownership_events = {
	to_exarch_effect = {
		EFFECT = "country_event = { id = nhs2_ely_marches.3 days = 1 }"
	}
}

to_transfer_provinces_to_exarch = {
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			nhs_$TAG$_province = yes
			NOT = { has_province_flag = nhs_exarch_province_exemption }
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = to_varangian_headquarters }
			NOT = { is_core = ROOT }
			NOT = { is_territorial_core = ROOT }
			NOT = { has_construction = core }
			NOT = { has_construction = missionary }
			is_owned_by_trade_company = no
			OR = {
				owned_by = ROOT
				owner = {
					tag = ELG
					is_subject_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			NOT = { has_province_modifier = nhs2_supply_lines_tm }
		}
		to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
			CURRENT_OWNER = owner
			NEW_OWNER = $TAG$
		}
	}
}

to_add_core_and_release_exarch = {
	hidden_effect = {
		# tooltip = {
		# 	cede_province = $TAG$
		# }
		add_core = $TAG$
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_core = ROOT
			}
			remove_core = ROOT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_part_of_hre = yes
			}
			set_in_empire = no
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_claim = ROOT
			}
			remove_claim = ROOT
		}
		# set_province_flag = to_ignore_triumph_check
		ROOT = {
			release = $TAG$
		}
		# clr_province_flag = to_ignore_triumph_check
	}
}

to_handle_exarch_autonomy_modifier = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				to_has_exarch_government_reform = yes
			}
			NOT = { culture_group = byzantine }
		}
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = to_exarch_autonomy_penalty
			duration = -1
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
}

to_handle_exarch_change_capital = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			owner = {
				to_has_exarch_government_reform = yes
				NOT = { primary_culture = PREV }
			}
		}
		owner = {
			change_primary_culture = PREV
		}
	}
}

to_setup_exarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			NOT = { government = republic }
		}
		change_government = republic
	}
	add_government_reform = to_exarch_reform
	if = {
		limit = {
			always = yes
			[[DO_NOT_SET_PRIMARY_CULTURE] always = no ]
		}
		capital_scope = {
			PREV = {
				change_primary_culture = PREV
			}
		}
	}
}

to_setup_greek_exarch = {
	to_setup_exarch = { DO_NOT_SET_PRIMARY_CULTURE = yes }
	change_primary_culture = greek
}

to_setup_anatolia_exarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = to_orhans_descendant_rules_anatolia
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { government = monarchy }
			}
			change_government = monarchy
		}
		change_primary_culture = turkish
		define_ruler = {
			dynasty = "Osmanoglu"
			male = yes
			culture = turkish
			hide_skills = yes
			claim = 95
		}
		add_government_reform = to_exarch_reform_monarchy_locked_dynasty
	}
	else = {
		to_setup_exarch = { DO_NOT_SET_PRIMARY_CULTURE = yes }
		change_primary_culture = turkish
	}
}

to_setup_anatolia_exarch_tooltip = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = to_orhans_descendant_rules_anatolia
		}
		custom_tooltip = to_set_exarch_reform_monarchy_keep_dynasty_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_tooltip = to_set_exarch_reform_republic_tt
	}
}

to_setup_illyris_exarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = to_kastrioti_rule_albania
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { government = monarchy }
			}
			change_government = monarchy
		}
		change_primary_culture = shqipproi
		define_ruler = {
			dynasty = "Kastrioti"
			male = yes
			culture = shqipproi
			hide_skills = yes
			claim = 95
		}
		add_government_reform = to_exarch_reform_monarchy_locked_dynasty
	}
	else = {
		to_setup_exarch = {}
	}
}

to_setup_illyris_exarch_tooltip = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			has_global_flag = to_kastrioti_rule_albania
		}
		custom_tooltip = to_set_exarch_reform_monarchy_keep_dynasty_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_tooltip = to_set_exarch_reform_republic_tt
	}
}

to_transfer_province_or_create_exarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			$EXARCH_SCOPE$ = {
				exists = yes
			}
		}
		to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
			CURRENT_OWNER = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			NEW_OWNER = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			$EXARCH_SCOPE$ = {
				exists = no
			}
		}
		to_release_exarch_from_province = {
			EXARCH_SCOPE = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
			CURRENT_OWNER = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		to_setup_exarch_government_and_transfer_provinces = {
			EXARCH_SCOPE = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
			EXARCH_TAG = $EXARCH_TAG$
			OVERLORD = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			ON_CREATED_EFFECT = $ON_CREATED_EFFECT$
			ON_CREATED_TOOLTIP = $ON_CREATED_TOOLTIP$
		}
	}
}

to_release_exarch_from_province = {
	hidden_effect = {
		to_save_years_of_nationalism = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_part_of_hre = yes
			}
			set_in_empire = no
		}
		clr_province_flag = nhs_exarch_province_exemption

		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					PREV = {
						is_state_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			remove_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_state_core = $EXARCH_SCOPE$ }
				}
				add_core = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					PREV = {
						is_territorial_core = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			remove_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			set_province_flag = to_add_territorial_core
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					PREV = {
						is_permanent_claim = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			set_province_flag = to_add_permanent_claim
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					PREV = {
						is_claim = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			set_province_flag = to_add_claim
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_core = $EXARCH_SCOPE$ }
			}
			set_province_flag = to_temp_core
			add_core = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}
		
		$CURRENT_OWNER$ = {
			release = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
			create_subject = {
				subject_type = elysian_subject
				subject = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
			}
			set_country_flag = to_created_exarch_@$EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = to_temp_core
			}
			clr_province_flag = to_temp_core
			remove_core = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = to_add_territorial_core
			}
			clr_province_flag = to_add_territorial_core
			add_territorial_core = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = to_add_permanent_claim
			}
			clr_province_flag = to_add_permanent_claim
			add_permanent_claim = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = to_add_claim
			}
			clr_province_flag = to_add_claim
			add_claim = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
		}
		set_province_flag = to_separatism_restore_pending
		province_event = { id = nhs2_ely_marches.5 days = 1 }
		to_load_years_of_nationalism = yes
	}
}

to_setup_exarch_government_and_transfer_provinces = {
	hidden_effect = {
		$EXARCH_SCOPE$ = {
			change_religion = $OVERLORD$
			to_set_unit_type = yes
			swap_free_idea_group = yes
			
			$ON_CREATED_EFFECT$

			set_ruler_culture = THIS

			add_republican_tradition = 100
			add_republican_tradition = -20
			add_adm_power = 200
			add_dip_power = 200
			add_mil_power = 200
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { prestige = 15 }
				}
				add_prestige = 20
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { treasury = 100 }
				}
				add_treasury = 150
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { manpower = 3 }
				}
				add_manpower = 5
			}
		}
	
		to_transfer_exarch_provinces = {
			EXARCH_SCOPE = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
			EXARCH_TAG = $EXARCH_TAG$
			OVERLORD_SCOPE = $OVERLORD$
		}
	}
	
	custom_tooltip = to_exarch_starting_land_$EXARCH_TAG$_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_exarch_creation_starting_land_limits_tt
	custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt
	
	$EXARCH_SCOPE$ = {
		$ON_CREATED_TOOLTIP$
	}

	custom_tooltip = to_reform_effects_for_overlord_tt
	if = {
		limit = {
			$OVERLORD$ = {
				mission_completed = to_the_eagle_rises_mission
			}
		}
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_govcap_exarch_reduced_tt
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_forcelimit_exarch_reduced_tt
	}
	else = {
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_govcap_exarch_tt
		custom_tooltip = to_reduce_overlord_forcelimit_exarch_tt
	}
	custom_tooltip = to_exarch_bonus_merchant_tt
	custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt

	custom_tooltip = to_reform_effects_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_automatically_accepts_culture_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_min_autonomy_exarch_modifier_tt
	custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt

	custom_tooltip = to_reform_modifiers_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_exarch_reform_modifiers_tt
	custom_tooltip = nhs_new_line_tt

	custom_tooltip = to_reform_government_attributes_tt
	custom_tooltip = to_exarch_reform_government_attributes_tt
}

to_check_exarch_incorrect_province = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			OR = {
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = ELG }

				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEA }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEB }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEC }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EED }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEE }
	
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEF }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEG }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEH }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEI }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEJ }
	
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEL }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEM }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEO }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EER }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EES }
	
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EET }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEU }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEV }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEP }
				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEQ }

				nhs_exarch_province_owned_incorrectly = { EXARCH_TAG = EEY }
			}
		}
		owner = {
			overlord = {
				ROOT = {
					cede_province = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_transfer_exarch_provinces = {
	$EXARCH_SCOPE$ = {
		overlord = {
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = PREV
					[[PROVINCE_TRIGGER]
					$PROVINCE_TRIGGER$
					]
					[[EXARCH_TAG]
					nhs_$EXARCH_TAG$_province = yes
					]
					to_exarch_can_get_province_passive = yes
				}
				to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
					CURRENT_OWNER = $OVERLORD_SCOPE$
					NEW_OWNER = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ELG = {
					exists = yes
					NOT = { tag = $EXARCH_SCOPE$ }
					overlord = {
						overlord_of = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
					}
				}
			}
			ELG = {
				every_province = {
					limit = {
						owned_by = PREV
						[[PROVINCE_TRIGGER]
						$PROVINCE_TRIGGER$
						]
						[[EXARCH_TAG]
						nhs_$EXARCH_TAG$_province = yes
						]
						to_exarch_can_get_province_passive = yes
					}
					to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
						CURRENT_OWNER = ELG
						NEW_OWNER = $EXARCH_SCOPE$
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_remove_exarch_cores = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject = yes
			is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
		}
		country_event = { id = nhs2_ely_marches.4 }
	}
}

to_cede_province_to_exarch = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_part_of_hre = yes
		}
		set_in_empire = no
	}
	clr_province_flag = nhs_exarch_province_exemption
	to_save_years_of_nationalism = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_state_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		if = {
			limit = {
				$NEW_OWNER$ = {
					PREV = {
						previous_owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			cede_province = EEZ
		}
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_state_core = $NEW_OWNER$ }
			}
			add_core = $NEW_OWNER$
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_territorial_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		if = {
			limit = {
				$NEW_OWNER$ = {
					PREV = {
						previous_owner = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			cede_province = EEZ
		}
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		add_territorial_core = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_permanent_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		add_permanent_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		add_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	else = {
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		# Province can have a core and a claim at the same time, but it would look weird in the tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_permanent_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			}
			remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			add_permanent_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			}
			remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			add_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
		}
	}
	set_province_flag = to_separatism_restore_pending
	hidden_effect = {
		province_event = { id = nhs2_ely_marches.5 days = 1 }
	}
	to_load_years_of_nationalism = yes
}

to_cede_province_to_exarch_overlord = {
	set_province_flag = nhs_exarch_province_exemption
	to_save_years_of_nationalism = yes
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_state_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_state_core = $NEW_OWNER$ }
			}
			add_core = $NEW_OWNER$
		}
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_territorial_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_core = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		add_territorial_core = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_permanent_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		add_permanent_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = {
			is_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		}
		remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
		add_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	else = {
		cede_province = $NEW_OWNER$
	}
	hidden_effect = {
		# Province can have a core and a claim at the same time, but it would look weird in the tooltip
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_permanent_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			}
			remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			add_permanent_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			}
			remove_claim = $CURRENT_OWNER$
			add_claim = $NEW_OWNER$
		}
	}
	set_province_flag = to_separatism_restore_pending
	hidden_effect = {
		province_event = { id = nhs2_ely_marches.5 days = 1 }
	}
	to_load_years_of_nationalism = yes
}

to_exarch_merchant_effect_from_province = {
	# Code generated by exarchs/exarch_generation.py
	if = {
		limit = { nhs_EEA_province = yes }
		EEA = { $EFFECT$ }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { nhs_EEB_province = yes }
		EEB = { $EFFECT$ }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { nhs_EEC_province = yes }
		EEC = { $EFFECT$ }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { nhs_EED_province = yes }
		EED = { $EFFECT$ }
	}
	else_if = {
		limit = { nhs_EEE_province = yes }
		EEE = { $EFFECT$ }
	}

to_check_exarch_claims_check_all_provinces = {
	every_owned_province = {
		set_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@$EXARCH_TAG$
		every_neighbor_province = {
			set_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@$EXARCH_TAG$
		}
		every_neighbor_sea_zone = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				set_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@$EXARCH_TAG$
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_claims_on_province_gained = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_city = yes
			owner = {
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
			}
		}
		set_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@ROOT
		every_neighbor_province = {
			set_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@ROOT
		}
		every_neighbor_sea_zone = {
			every_neighbor_province = {
				set_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@ROOT
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_claims_on_province_lost = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_city = yes
			FROM = {
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
			}
		}
		every_province = {
			clr_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			to_check_exarch_claims_check_all_provinces = { EXARCH_TAG = FROM }
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_claims_on_become_subject = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
		}
		every_province = {
			clr_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim@FROM
		}
		to_check_exarch_claims_check_all_provinces = { EXARCH_TAG = FROM }
	}
}

to_fabricate_exarch_claim_effect = {
	if = {
		limit = {
			$EXARCH_TAG$ = {
				is_subject_of = ROOT
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim$EXARCH_TAG$
			}
		}
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_flag = nhs_eligible_for_exarch_claim$EXARCH_TAG$
				NOT = { is_claim = $EXARCH_TAG$ }
				NOT = { is_permanent_claim = $EXARCH_TAG$ }
			}
			add_claim = $EXARCH_TAG$
		}
	}
}

to_initialize_custom_exarch_peripheral_territories = {
	set_variable = {
		which = to_custom_exarch_province_cost
		value = 0
	}
	set_variable = {
		which = to_custom_exarch_province_local_cost
		value = 0
	}
	every_province = {
		limit = {
			owned_by = PREV
			$PROVINCE_TRIGGER$
		}
		PREV = {
			set_country_flag = to_exarch_has_peripheral_territories
		}
		set_province_flag = to_exarch_permanently_owned_land_@PREV
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { to_potential_exarch_province = yes }
			}
			PREV = {
				change_variable = {
					which = to_custom_exarch_province_cost
					value = 5
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			to_exarch_merchant_effect_from_province = {
				EFFECT = "
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant
					value = -1
				}
				"
			}
			to_exarch_merchant_2_effect_from_province = {
				EFFECT = "
				change_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_needed_provinces_for_merchant_2
					value = -1
				}
				"
			}
		}
	}
	if = {
		limit = {
			check_variable = {
				which = to_custom_exarch_province_cost
				value = 501
			}
		}
		set_variable = {
			which = to_custom_exarch_province_cost
			value = 500
		}
	}
	# else_if = {
	# 	limit = {
	# 		NOT = {
	# 			check_variable = {
	# 				which = to_custom_exarch_province_cost
	# 				value = 50
	# 			}
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# 	set_variable = {
	# 		which = to_custom_exarch_province_cost
	# 		value = 50
	# 	}
	# }
}

to_monthly_exarch_modifiers_check = {
	nhs_effect_for_existing_elysian_tag = {
		EFFECT = "
		to_check_exarch_modifier_all_subjects = { MODIFIER_NAME = nationalism MODIFIER = years_of_nationalism }
		to_check_exarch_modifier_all_subjects = { MODIFIER_NAME = coring_cost MODIFIER = core_creation }
		to_check_exarch_modifier_all_subjects = { MODIFIER_NAME = admin_efficiency MODIFIER = administrative_efficiency }
		"
	}
}

to_check_exarch_modifier_all_subjects = {
	hidden_effect = {
		every_subject_country = {
			limit = {
				to_has_exarch_government_reform = yes
			}
			to_check_exarch_modifier = {
				MODIFIER_NAME = $MODIFIER_NAME$
				MODIFIER = $MODIFIER$
				[[MODIFY]
				MODIFY = $MODIFY$
				]
			}
		}
	}
}

to_check_exarch_modifier = {
	hidden_effect = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_subject_of_type = elysian_subject
				to_has_exarch_government_reform = yes
			}
			overlord = {
				PREV = {
					export_to_variable = {
						which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff
						value = modifier:$MODIFIER$
						who = PREV
					}
				}
			}
			export_to_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$
				value = modifier:$MODIFIER$
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff_previous
							value = 0
						}
					}
				}
				subtract_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$
					which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff_previous
				}
			}
			subtract_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff
				which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$
			}
			[[MODIFY]
			subtract_variable = {
				which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff
				value = $MODIFY$
			}
			]
			to_round_down_variable_two_decimals = {
				VARIABLE = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						is_variable_equal = {
							which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff
							which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff_previous
						}
					}
				}
				to_add_correct_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_modifier = yes
				set_variable = {
					which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff_previous
					which = to_exarch_$MODIFIER_NAME$_diff
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

to_add_correct_exarch_nationalism_modifier = {
	# Code generated by exarchs/exarch_modifier_copies.py
	if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=0.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=25.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=38.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=44.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=47.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=49.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=50.0}}if = {limit={NOT={has_country_modifier=to_exarch_nationalism_100}} to_remove_exarch_nationalism_modifiers=yes add_country_modifier={name=to_exarch_nationalism_100 duration=-1 hidden = yes} }}else={if = {limit={NOT={has_country_modifier=to_exarch_nationalism_99}} to_remove_exarch_nationalism_modifiers=yes add_country_modifier={name=to_exarch_nationalism_99 duration=-1 hidden = yes} }}}else={if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=48.0}}if = {limit={NOT={has_country_modifier=to_exarch_nationalism_98}} to_remove_exarch_nationalism_modifiers=yes add_country_modifier={name=to_exarch_nationalism_98 duration=-1 hidden = yes} }}else={if = {limit={NOT={has_country_modifier=to_exarch_nationalism_97}} to_remove_exarch_nationalism_modifiers=yes add_country_modifier={name=to_exarch_nationalism_97 duration=-1 hidden = yes} }}}}else={if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=45.0}}if={limit={check_variable={which=to_exarch_nationalism_diff value=46.0}}if =
